<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>IT
Tech Packaging, Inc. Announces Fourth Quarter and Fiscal Year 2023 Financial Results</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">BAODING,&nbsp;China,&nbsp;March
27, 2024&nbsp;/PRNewswire/ --&nbsp;IT Tech Packaging, Inc. (NYSE American: ITP) (&ldquo;IT Tech Packaging&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;),
a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products in&nbsp;North China, today announced its unaudited financial results
for the fourth&nbsp;quarter&nbsp;and audited financial results for the fiscal year&nbsp;ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Mr.
Zhenyong Liu, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer of the Company, commented, &rdquo; In 2023, the company achieved a revenue of $86.55
million and a gross profit of $1.00 million. The overall performance improved due to slightly increased sales volume. Considering current
conditions, including supportive policies and the implementation of plastic-restriction-orders, we expect a rise in domestic demand for
packaging paper. In the long run, we will focus on acquiring new customers, reducing costs and improving efficiency and ensuring safe
and environmentally friendly production. Moreover, we plan to implement flexible pricing and inventory management in line with market
trends to maintain cash flow and minimize risks while achieving reasonable profit levels.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Fourth
Quarter 2023 Financial Results</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#9679;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
                                            decreased by 1.91% to&nbsp;approximately $20.96 million, primarily attributable to a decrease
                                            in the average selling price(&ldquo;ASP&rdquo;) of CMP, partially offset by an increase in
                                            sales volume of regular CMP, light-weight CMP and offset printing paper.</FONT></TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#9679;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Gross
                                            profit decreased by 75.61% to&nbsp;approximately $0.25 million. Total gross margin decreased
                                            by 3.61 percentage point to 1.19%.</FONT></TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#9679;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Loss
                                            from operations was&nbsp;approximately $3.80 million, compared to $0.49 million&nbsp;for
                                            the same period of previous year.</FONT></TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#9679;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Net
                                            loss was&nbsp;approximately $3.98 million, or loss of $0.40&nbsp;per basic and diluted share,
                                            compared to $11.91 million, or loss of&nbsp;$1.19&nbsp;per basic and diluted share, for the
                                            same period of previous year.</FONT></TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#9679;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Earnings
                                            before interest, taxes, depreciation and amortization (&ldquo;EBITDA&rdquo;) decreased by 97.08%
                                            to&nbsp;approximately $0.11 million.</FONT></TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Revenue</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">For
the fourth quarter of 2023, total revenue decreased by&nbsp;approximately $0.41 million, or 1.91%, to&nbsp;approximately $20.96 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately
$21.37 million&nbsp;for the same period of previous year. The decrease in total revenue was mainly due to the decrease in ASP of CMP
and offset printing paper, partially offset by increase in sales volume of regular CMP, light-weight CMP and offset printing paper.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: normal 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from CMP, including both regular CMP and light-Weight CMP, decreased by&nbsp;$0.58 million, or 2.78%, to&nbsp;approximately $20.46 million&nbsp;and
accounted for 97.62 % of total revenue for the fourth quarter of 2023, compared to&nbsp;approximately $21.05 million, or 98.49% of total
revenue, for the same period of previous year. The Company sold 56,805 tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$360/tonne in the fourth quarter
of 2023, compared to 51,306 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$410/tonne in the same period of previous year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Of
the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP decreased by&nbsp;approximately $0.26 million, or 1.52%, to&nbsp;approximately $17.02 million,
resulting from sales of 46,958 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$362/tonne, during the fourth quarter of 2023, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately$17.28
million, resulting from sales of 41,941 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$412/tonne, for the same period of previous year. Revenue from light-weight
CMP decreased by&nbsp;approximately $0.32 million, or 8.54%, to&nbsp;approximately $3.45 million, resulting from sales of 9,847 tonnes
at an ASP of&nbsp;$350/tonne for the fourth quarter of 2023, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $3.77 million, resulting from
sales of 9,365 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$402/tonne for the same period of previous year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from offset printing paper was $nil for the three months ended December 31, 2023 and 2022, respectively.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from tissue paper products increased by&nbsp;$0.22 million, or 87.04%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.47 million, resulting from sales of 480
tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$987/tonne, for the fourth quarter of 2023, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately$0.25million, resulting
from sales of 234 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,083/tonne for the same period of previous year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from face masks decreased by&nbsp;$45,791, or 80.65%, to&nbsp;approximately $10,983&nbsp;&nbsp;for the fourth quarter ended&nbsp;December
31, 2023, from $56,774 for the same period of 2022. The Company sold 360 thousand pieces of face masks for the fourth quarter ended&nbsp;December
31, 2023, compared to 1,330 thousand pieces of face masks for the same period of 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Gross
Profit and Gross Margin</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Total
cost of sales increased by&nbsp;$0.37 million, or 1.81%, to&nbsp;approximately $20.71 million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2023 from&nbsp;approximately
$20.34 million&nbsp;for the same period of previous year. For paper products, overall cost of sales per tonne was&nbsp;$361&nbsp;for
the fourth quarter of 2023, compared to&nbsp;$394&nbsp;for the same period of previous year. Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP,
light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, and tissue paper products were&nbsp;$343,&nbsp;$331,&nbsp;$nil and&nbsp;$2,785, respectively,
for the fourth quarter of 2023, compared to&nbsp;&nbsp;$378,&nbsp;$361,&nbsp;$nil and&nbsp;$4,494, respectively, for the same period
of previous year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Total
gross profit was&nbsp;approximately $0.25 million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2023, compare to the gross profit of&nbsp;approximately
$1.03 million&nbsp;for the same period of previous year as a result of factors described above. Overall gross margin was 1.19% for the
fourth quarter of 2023, compared to 4.8% for the same period of previous year. Gross profit (loss) margins for regular CMP, light-weight
CMP, offset printing paper, tissue paper products and face mask products were 5.32%, 5.50%, 41.02%, -182.10% and -21.19%, respectively,
for the fourth quarter of 2023, compared to 8.28%, 10.28%, n/a, -315.16% and 27.47%, respectively, for the same period of previous year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

General and Administrative Expenses</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Selling,

the fourth quarter of 2023 from&nbsp;approximately $1.52 million&nbsp;for the same period of previous year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

(Loss) from Operations</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Loss
from operations was&nbsp;approximately $3.80 million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2023, an increase of $3.31 million, or 673.41%, from
$0.49 million&nbsp;for the same period of previous year. Operating loss margin was 18.13% for the fourth quarter of 2023, 2.30% for the
same period of previous year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

Income (Loss)</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

a decrease of $7.92 million, or 66.54%, from $11.91 million, or&nbsp;$1.19 loss&nbsp;per basic and diluted share, for the same period
of previous year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>EBITDA</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: left; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">EBITDA
was&nbsp;approximately $0.11 million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter of 2023, compared to&nbsp;approximately $3.77 million&nbsp;for the same
period of previous year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Note
1: Non-GAAP Financial Measures</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">In
addition to our U.S. GAAP results, this press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the
Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;). The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation
and amortization. EBITDA is a key measure used by management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes
this measure is useful to investors because it is an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations,
the Company&rsquo;s presentation of EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed
as an alternative to measures of financial performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Reconciliation
of Net Income to EBITDA</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>(Amounts
expressed in US$)</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Revenue</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">For
the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023, total revenue decreased by&nbsp;$13.81 million, or 13.76%, to&nbsp;approximately $86.55 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately
$100.35 million&nbsp;for 2022. The decrease in total revenue was mainly due to the decrease in average selling price (&ldquo;ASP&rdquo;)
of CMP, partially offset by increase in sales volume of regular CMP, light-weight CMP and offset printing paper .</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from CMP, including both regular CMP and light-Weight CMP decreased by&nbsp;$16.83 million, or 17.05%, to&nbsp;approximately $81.89 million,
and accounted for 94.62% of total revenue for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023, compared to approximately $98.73 million, or 98.38%
of total revenue for 2022. The Company sold 223,823 tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$366/tonne in the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023,
compared to 218,331 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$452/tonne in 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Of
the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP decreased by&nbsp;$14.93 million, or 18.14%, to&nbsp;approximately $67.37 million, resulting
from sales of 182,870 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$368/tonne during the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately
$82.30 million, resulting from sales of 180,977 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$455/tonne for 2022. Revenue from light-weight CMP decreased
by&nbsp;$1.91 million, or 11.61%, to&nbsp;approximately$14.52 million, resulting from sales of 40,953 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$355/tonne
for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $16.43 million, resulting from sales of 37,354 tonnes
at an ASP of&nbsp;$440/tonne for 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from offset printing paper was $3.22 for the year ended December 31, 2023. Due to COVID-19, our paper production was restricted and production
of offset printing paper was suspended in 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from tissue paper products decreased by&nbsp;$0.05 million, or 3.76%, to&nbsp;approximately $1.31 million, resulting from sales of 1,205
tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,083/tonne, for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $1.36 million,
resulting from sales of 1,273 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,065/tonne for 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Revenue
from face masks decreased by&nbsp;$0.15 million, or 58.86%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.11 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December
31, 2023, from approximately $0.26 million for 2022. The Company sold 3,383 thousand pieces of face masks for the year ended&nbsp;December
31, 2023, compared to 5,625 thousand pieces of face masks for 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Gross
Profit and Gross Margin</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Total
cost of sales decreased by $10.05 million, or 10.51%, to&nbsp;approximately $85.55 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31,
2023&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $95.60 million&nbsp;for 2022. The decrease in overall cost of sales was mainly due to due to the decrease
of material costs of CMP in the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023.&nbsp; Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight CMP,
offset printing paper, tissue paper products were,&nbsp;$349,&nbsp;$345,&nbsp;$563, and&nbsp;$3,584, respectively, for the year ended&nbsp;December
31, 2023&nbsp;compared to&nbsp;$421, $398, $nil, and $3,370 respectively, for 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Total
gross profit decreased by&nbsp;$3.75 million, or 78.97%, to&nbsp;approximately $1.00 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31,
2023&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $4.75 million&nbsp;for 2022. Overall gross margin decreased by 3.58 percentage points to 1.16% for
the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023&nbsp;from 4.74% for 2022. Gross margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper,
tissue paper products and face mask products were 5.27%, 2.59%, 2.41, -230.86% and -10.49%, respectively, for the year ended&nbsp;December
31, 2023, compared to 7.39%, 9.42%, nil, -216.34% and 26.11%, respectively, for 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Selling,
General and Administrative Expenses</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">SG&amp;A
expenses decreased by&nbsp;$0.98 million, or 9.78%, to&nbsp;approximately $9.08 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately
$10.06 million&nbsp;for 2022. As a percentage of total revenue, SG&amp;A expenses was 10.45% for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023,
compared to 10.02% for 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Income
(Loss) from Operations</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Loss
from operations decreased by&nbsp;$4.27million, or 80.52% to&nbsp;approximately $9.58 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31,
2023&nbsp;from $5.30 million&nbsp;for 2022. Operating loss margin was 11.06% for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023, compared to 5.29%
for 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Net
Income (Loss)</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Net
loss increased by&nbsp;$6.63 million, or 39.98%, to&nbsp;approximately $9.95 million, or loss per basic and diluted share of&nbsp;$0.99,
for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023, compared to net loss of&nbsp;approximately $16.57 million, or loss per basic and diluted share
of&nbsp;$1.66 for 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>EBITDA</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">EBITDA
decreased by&nbsp;$5.35 million, or 48.81%, to&nbsp;approximately $5.61 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately
$10.96 million&nbsp;for 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Note
1: Non-GAAP Financial Measures</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">In
addition to our U.S. GAAP results, this press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the
Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;). The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation
and amortization. EBITDA is a key measure used by management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes
this measure is useful to investors because it is an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations,
the Company&rsquo;s presentation of EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed
as an alternative to measures of financial performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Reconciliation
of Net Income to EBITDA</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>(Amounts
expressed in US$)</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Cash,
Liquidity and Financial Position</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">As
of&nbsp;December 31, 2023, the Company had cash and bank balances, short-term debt (including bank loans, current portion of long-term
loans from credit union and related party loans), and long-term debt (including loan from credit union) of&nbsp;approximately $3.92&nbsp;million,&nbsp;$8.03&nbsp;million
and&nbsp;$4.50&nbsp;million, respectively, compared to&nbsp;&nbsp;approximately $9.52&nbsp;million,&nbsp;$11.16&nbsp;million and&nbsp;$4.20&nbsp;million,
respectively, at the end of 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Net
accounts receivable was&nbsp;approximately $0.58&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;December 31, 2023, compared to&nbsp;&nbsp;approximately $nil
million&nbsp;as of&nbsp;December 31, 2022. Net inventory was&nbsp;approximately $3.56&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;December 31, 2023, compared
to&nbsp;approximately $2.87 million&nbsp;at the end of 2022. As of&nbsp;December 31, 2023, the Company had current assets of&nbsp;approximately
$28.36 million and current liabilities of&nbsp;approximately $21.42&nbsp;million, resulting in a working capital of&nbsp;approximately
$6.94 million. This was compared to current assets of&nbsp;approximately $47.17&nbsp;million and current liabilities of&nbsp;approximately
$17.64 million, resulting in a working capital of&nbsp;approximately $29.53&nbsp;million at the end of 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Net
Cash provided by operating activities was&nbsp;approximately $12.87 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023, compared
to approximately $10.72 million&nbsp;for 2022. Net cash used in investing activities was&nbsp;approximately $22.24 million&nbsp;for the
year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023, compared to&nbsp;approximately $10.90 million&nbsp;for 2022. Net cash provided by financing activities
was&nbsp;approximately $4.41 million&nbsp;for the year ended&nbsp;December 31, 2023, compared to net cash used in financing activities
of&nbsp;approximately $0.88 million&nbsp;for 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>About
IT Tech Packaging, Inc.</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Founded
in 1996, IT Tech Packaging, Inc. is a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products and single-use face masks in&nbsp;North
China. Using recycled paper as its primary raw material (with the exception of its tissue paper products), ITP produces and distributes
three categories of paper products: corrugating medium paper, offset printing paper and tissue paper products. With production based
in Baoding and Xingtai in&nbsp;North China&rsquo;s&nbsp;Hebei Province, ITP is located strategically close to the&nbsp;Beijing&nbsp;and&nbsp;Tianjin&nbsp;region,
home to a growing base of industrial and manufacturing activities and one of the largest markets for paper products consumption in the
country. ITP has been listed on the NYSE American since&nbsp;December 2009. For more information, please visit:&nbsp;https://www.itpackaging.cn/.</FONT></P>
